   function addCss(fileName) {
		var link = '<link rel="stylesheet" type="text/css" href="' + fileName + '">';
		$j_1_11('head').append(link);
	}
	
	$j_1_11(function() {
		if (navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf('chrome') > -1){
			addCss('https://images.booksamillion.com/stylesheets/base_chrome_20170517.css');

  <script>
   $j_1_11(document).ready(function() {
		// AFTER the header ticker and CSS are loaded, show the ticker
		// That is, prevent display of all ticker content on initial render
		$j_1_11('div[class^="header-ticker"]').show();

		// reveal header menus on click, hide on re-click / click elsewhere
		$j_1_11('.header-menu').on("click keypress",
			function(event) { 
				event.stopPropagation();
				event.stopImmediatePropagation

				// Proceed ONLY if (an element within) a header menu element was clicked / pressed
				// BUT don't toggle if clicking WITHIN a header menu (category nav or store zip entry) ...
				if ($j_1_11(event.target).closest('.header-menu').length
				&&	$j_1_11(event.target).closest('#search-zip2').length == 0 && $j_1_11(event.target).closest('#category-nav-container').length == 0) {
					// turn OFF any existing body event handler
					$j_1_11('body').off("click keypress",closeHeaderMenus);

					// CLOSE any OTHER header menus
					closeHeaderMenus(event);

					// ADD a body event (click-off will close header menus) handler
					$j_1_11('body').on("click keypress",closeHeaderMenus);

					var menuContainerID = $j_1_11(event.target).closest('.header-menu').data('menucontainerid');
					if (menuContainerID == "store-info-container") {
					        // If Set My Store is set before auto-definition using IP / Location 
						// - show zip-code entry instead of undefined store details
        					if ( ! $j_1_11(".store_hdr_info").data("store-defined") ) {
            						$j_1_11("#search_help2").trigger( "click" );
            					//	return false;
						} else {
							storeInfoToHTML();
						}
					}
					$j_1_11('#' + menuContainerID).toggle();
				}
			},
		);

		// Setup the (browse by category) accordion
		$j_1_11(".accordian a").click(function(){
			var link = $j_1_11(this);
			var closest_ul = link.closest("ul");
			var parallel_active_links = closest_ul.find(".active")
			var closest_li = link.closest("li");
			var link_status = closest_li.hasClass("active");
			var count = 0;

			closest_ul.find("ul").slideUp(function(){
				if(++count == closest_ul.find("ul").length)
					parallel_active_links.removeClass("active");
			});

			if(!link_status) {
				closest_li.children("ul").slideDown('fast');
				closest_li.addClass("active");
			}
		});
		$j_1_11('.accordian .closer').on('click', function(event) { $j_1_11('.accordian').slideUp('fast') });

		$j_1_11('#filter').on("change", function() {
			if ("" == $j_1_11('#filter option:selected').val()) {
				$j_1_11('#filter-toggle > i').show('slow','fade');
				$j_1_11('.box').removeClass('search-expanded');
				$j_1_11('#filter-toggle').focus();
			} else {
				$j_1_11('#filter-toggle > i').hide();
			}
		});

		$j_1_11('#searchIcon').on("click keypress", function() {
			document.forms['search'].submit();
		});

		// on initial page load - show active filter, if any
		if ("" != $j_1_11('#filter option:selected').val()) {
			$j_1_11('.box').addClass('search-expanded');
			$j_1_11('#filter-toggle > i').hide();
		}

	}); // document.ready

	function closeHeaderMenus(event) {
		var retain = $j_1_11(event.target).closest('.header-menu').find('.header-menu-container');

		// header menu clicked - (keep) open, close others
		if (retain.length) {
				$j_1_11('.box').find('.header-menu-container').not(retain).slideUp('fast');

		// no header menu clicked, close ALL header menus
		} else {
			$j_1_11('body').off("click keypress",closeHeaderMenus);
			$j_1_11('.header-menu-container').slideUp('fast');
		}
	}

	// show | hide the search filter
	function toggleFilter() {
		if (!$j_1_11('.search-filter').is(":visible")) { // maybe .box hasClass(.search-expanded) is better, maybe worse?
			$j_1_11('#filter-toggle i').replaceWith('<i class="material-icons">keyboard_arrow_right</i>');
			$j_1_11('.box').addClass('search-expanded');
			$j_1_11('#filter').focus();
		} else {
			$j_1_11('#filter-toggle i').replaceWith('<i class="material-icons">keyboard_arrow_down</i>');
			$j_1_11('.box').removeClass('search-expanded');
			$j_1_11('#filter-toggle').focus();
		}
	}
  </script>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        //Validate email before sending to LISTRAK
						$j_1_11(document).ready(function() {
							$j_1_11('#newsletter-footer-form').submit(function(e) {
								var sEmail = $j_1_11('#footerEmail').val();
								// Checking Empty Fields First
								if ($j_1_11.trim(sEmail).length == 0) {
									e.preventDefault();
									$j_1_11('.emailError').html("Email field can not be blank!");
									return false;
								} else if (!validateEmail(sEmail)) {
									e.preventDefault();
									$j_1_11('.emailError').html("Invalid email address!");
									return false;
								} else {
									return true;
								}
							});
						});
						
						function validateEmail(sEmail) {
							var filter = /^[a-z0-9_\-.\+]+\@[a-z0-9.-]+\.[a-z0-9]{2,4}$/i;
							if (filter.test(sEmail)) {
								return true;
							} else {
								return false;
							}
						}
						
						$j_1_11( window ).resize(function() {
							var windowWidth = $j_1_11( window ).width();
							if (windowWidth < 700) {
								$j_1_11(".footerColHeader").parent().children("div").hide();
							} else {
								$j_1_11(".footerColHeader").parent().children("div").show();
							}
						});
						
						$j_1_11(document).ready(function() {
							$j_1_11(".footerColHeader").on("click", function(e) {
								if ( $j_1_11(window).width() <= 700 ) {
									var footBasis = $j_1_11(this).closest("div").css("flex-basis");       
									if (footBasis === "100%") { 
										$j_1_11(this).closest("div").children("div").toggle( "slide", { direction: "up" }, "slow" );
										$j_1_11(this).closest("div").css("flex-basis","40%");
									} else {
										$j_1_11(this).closest("div").css("flex-basis","100%");
										$j_1_11(this).closest("div").children("div").toggle( "slide", { direction: "down" }, "slow" );
									};
								};
							});
						});
       </script>

  <!-- Lazy Loader -->
  <script>
   function lazyInit() {
                var imgDefer = document.getElementsByTagName('img');
                for (var i=0; i<imgDefer.length; i++) {
                                if(imgDefer[i].getAttribute('data-src')) {
                                imgDefer[i].setAttribute('src',imgDefer[i].getAttribute('data-src'));
} } }
window.onload = lazyInit;
  </script>
